        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer365826657" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14806284128348548117">HOLYYYYY OH MY GOD THIS WAS AMAZING I CANNOT FORM SENTENCES OMG THIS WAS SOOOO GOOOOOODDD! AHH I EVEN CRIED OMGGGG<br/><br/>----------------*After spaz attack*-------------------<br/><br/><i>That Wedding</i> was holy crap amazing. I loved it so so so much! Ahh. It had me laughing, crying and everything in between. I cannot describe this awesomeness. I cannot praise Jillian Dodd enough. This was such a good book.<br/><br/>It’s been a while since I read <i>That Boy</i>, so I had totally forgotten how awesome it is to read Jillian Dodd’s wri</span>
  <span id="freeText14806284128348548117" style="display:none">HOLYYYYY OH MY GOD THIS WAS AMAZING I CANNOT FORM SENTENCES OMG THIS WAS SOOOO GOOOOOODDD! AHH I EVEN CRIED OMGGGG<br /><br />----------------*After spaz attack*-------------------<br /><br /><i>That Wedding</i> was holy crap amazing. I loved it so so so much! Ahh. It had me laughing, crying and everything in between. I cannot describe this awesomeness. I cannot praise Jillian Dodd enough. This was such a good book.<br /><br />It’s been a while since I read <i>That Boy</i>, so I had totally forgotten how awesome it is to read Jillian Dodd’s writing and how awesome JJ is. I loved every singly bit of That Wedding. It made me feel happy inside. <br /><br />Finally, JJ and Phillip are together! Yayayay! Now, they must work together to plan a kick-ass wedding. (Which they totally do!). Together, and with the help of close friends and family, JJ and Phillip form an even stronger bond and eventually get the blessing of Danny’s parents, Phillip’s parents and the Pastor. But, it is not without hardship. They discover new things about each other, and JJ freaks out because she thinks they are failing couple’s counselling. But, oh my God, this was a perfect book and they are perfect for each other!!!!!!<br /><br />So, yeah, I really loved this book, a lot! There was a lot of sex in this book, but Jillian Dodd was very shy on details. I have no problem with sex scenes in books, don’t get me wrong, but with the amount of sex in <i>That Wedding</i>, I was happy with how Jillian Dodd wrote it. <br /><br />The wedding was so perfect. I want to plan a wedding were everything just falls into place, just like JJ’s. Everything was so amazing and the descriptions were perfect. I even started crying a little bit! I cry a lot when I read books, I’m so lame, right? <br /><br />I was devastated when the book ended! I didn’t realise it at first, I just wanted it to go on forever. I’m so glad my friend, Georgie, got me to buy the <i>That Boy</i> ebook. This series is so great. I keep seeing things about a third book, <i>That Baby</i>… Really??? I am so excited about that, oh my gosh, I hope Phillip and JJ have like a thousand kids &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14806284128348548117" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText18071373547852213404" style="display:none">Before I start I have to say that I think That Boy was absolutely perfect and is a great stand alone book :)<br /><br />I knew before I even started That Wedding it would not be as good as the first book, because what happens after two people have already become a couple and engaged!? no excitement and no angst, that's what happens. And I was right! this book is literally is all about the wedding. (which I guess is okay since it <i>is</i> called <b>That Wedding</b>)<br /><br />One of the main things that bothered me was Phillip and JJ were not the same compared to how they were in the first book. JJ constantly mopes, cries, gets depressed, etc. but she would never do that in the first book. I also kept noticing moments where Phillip would say or do something the Phillip in the first book would definitely not do, like <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[getting pissed off when JJ was trying to reason with him that spending $5,000 on car modifications is way too much especially when they have very little budget for their wedding <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />They also have a lot of sex. And it usually plays out like this:<br /><br />-kissing-<br /><br />-takes off clothes-<br /><br />*I turn the page*<br /><br />-JJ saying something along the lines of "wow that was amazing"<br /><br /><i>end scene</i><br /><br />I mean that's great and everything but not when it happens multiple times in every other chapter..<br /><br />I stopped reading at about 40% and only because I literally fell asleep(and it was the middle of the day), but even though this book was not my cup of tea it doesn't take away how great the first book was :)<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

        rated it

              <span id="reviewTextContainer275930348" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15767366661204558316">Okay, first of all I have to say that I really enjoyed That Boy and that I think Jillian Dodd is a very talented writer. However, the format that she used in That Boy did not work in the sequel That Wedding. Why? Because there was really not much to be told in That Wedding. All you have is Jayden planning a wedding, Jayden freaking out and having second thoughts in relation to Phillip, and Jayden and Phillip having sex every other page. That is it! It gets pretty repetitive and it made me loathe</span>
  <span id="freeText15767366661204558316" style="display:none">Okay, first of all I have to say that I really enjoyed That Boy and that I think Jillian Dodd is a very talented writer. However, the format that she used in That Boy did not work in the sequel That Wedding. Why? Because there was really not much to be told in That Wedding. All you have is Jayden planning a wedding, Jayden freaking out and having second thoughts in relation to Phillip, and Jayden and Phillip having sex every other page. That is it! It gets pretty repetitive and it made me loathe Jayden's character. I liked her in That Boy. In That Wedding she just turned into an insensitive bitch. It also made me think that she shouldn't be getting married to Phillip, at least not at 22. She acts like a 14 year old all the time and if this was real life, their marriage wouldn't last a year.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15767366661204558316" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText12570286196330277402" style="display:none">This took me forever to finish.<br />Pros: <br />1) Phillip &amp; Danny. <br />2)Danny telling the mc off the way I wanted to tell her off.<br />3)The cover actually ties into the story.<br />Cons: <br />Everything. I don't even want to read the next book in this series but I am only doing it for Phillip... <br />I just hope it isn't as bad as this one. <br />I am extremely disappointed at everything that happened here...</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('KfBoTU8AWm1q7iQaZMkxN1OgVVAFUFnIi2zYcij+90tzduothR+eM4SHN3Pztab5692HP+bfcotfAPF82l3XAg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AO6CB3T0jG8VpANxxYu38xGNfUzw0NRxX3n+s4katytaaABnvutIMfvNEBhS9yA9qfCvIxNf/zKLFde9e7mXYg==')})
  }

Scott, crafts her signature heartfelt style into a brand new emotional, second chance, standalone romance. \n\n\nI have three goals: graduate from an Ivy League university, get into medical school, and follow in my father’s well-established footsteps. Everything was going exactly as planned until the local bad boy was delivered to my doorstep. Literally.\n\nFrom the moment we meet, my old life becomes unrecognizable, but I have no regrets. I’m utterly captivated by him. His smirk. His heart. His sharp wit.   <span id="freeText10042892999302675366" style="display:none">Jillian is a <i>USA TODAY</i> bestselling author who writes fun romance novels with characters her readers fall in love with--from the boy next door in the That Boy trilogy, to the daughter of a famous actress in The Keatyn Chronicles®, to a kick-ass young assassin in the Spy Girl® series. Jillian's books have enthralled more than two million readers since she burst onto the indie scene in 2011.<br /><br />She lives in a small Florida beach town, is married to her college sweetheart, has two grown children, and two Labrador Retrievers named Cali and Camber. When she's not working, she likes to travel, paint, shop for shoes, watch football, and go to the beach.<br /><br />Check out Jillian’s website for added content: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jilliandodd.net">www.jilliandodd.net</a><br /><br /></span>
